 \"text\": \"The SharedInformer factory and cache sync mechanism in kubernetes/kubernetes (and kubernetes/client-go) is implemented across several interconnected packages:\\n\\n## Core Cache Infrastructure (tools/cache/)\\n\\n**shared_informer.go** — The heart of the implementation. Defines the `SharedInformer` and `SharedIndexInformer` interfaces, and `sharedIndexInformer` struct which embeds a `controller`, a local `indexer` (store), and a `sharedProcessor` for fan-out event delivery. Key functions: `NewSharedIndexInformer`, `WaitForCacheSync`, `WaitForNamedCacheSync`. The `Run()` method starts the controller and processor; `HasSynced()` delegates to the underlying controller/DeltaFIFO.\\n\\n**controller.go** — Defines the `Controller` interface and its `controller` implementation. `controller.Run()` creates a `Reflector`, runs it against a `DeltaFIFO`, and runs `processLoop()` which calls `Pop` on the DeltaFIFO, dispatching to `ProcessFunc` (which is `sharedIndexInformer.HandleDeltas`). `processDeltas()` applies add/update/delete events to the local store and notifies handlers.\\n\\n**reflector.go** — Implements `Reflector` which drives the list-watch loop. `ListAndWatch()` does a full List to populate the store (via `DeltaFIFO.Replace`), then enters a Watch loop streaming incremental events. Handles resync, resource version management, and bookmark tracking.\\n\\n**listwatch.go** — Defines the `ListerWatcher` interface and `ListWatch` struct that wraps typed client functions. `NewListWatchFromClient` / `NewFilteredListWatchFromClient` build `ListWatch` objects from a typed REST client.\\n\\n**store.go** — Defines the `Store` interface and `cache` struct (the local in-memory store). `NewIndexer` creates an indexed store backed by `threadSafeMap`. `MetaNamespaceKeyFunc` is the default keying function.\\n\\n**thread_safe_store.go** — `ThreadSafeStore` / `threadSafeMap` provide the thread-safe in-memory map with secondary index support (`storeIndex`).\\n\\n**delta_fifo.go** — `DeltaFIFO` is the queue between the Reflector (producer) and the controller processLoop (consumer). `Replace()` does the initial sync from the List call; `Add/Update/Delete` handle watch events. `HasSynced()` tracks whether the initial list has been fully processed.\\n\\n**index.go** — Defines `Indexer` interface, `IndexFunc`, `MetaNamespaceIndexFunc`, `Indexers`, `Indices`, and `Index` types for secondary indexing.\\n\\n**synctrack/synctrack.go** — `AsyncTracker` and `SingleFileTracker` track per-item and global sync status, used by `sharedIndexInformer` to implement `HasSynced()`.\\n\\n## Factory Implementation (informers/)\\n\\n**informers/factory.go** — Implements `SharedInformerFactory` and the concrete `sharedInformerFactory`. `NewSharedInformerFactory` / `NewSharedInformerFactoryWithOptions` create the factory. `InformerFor()` registers or retrieves a `SharedIndexInformer` for a given object type, ensuring deduplication. `Start()` launches all registered informers. `WaitForCacheSync()` waits for all started informers to complete their initial list sync.\\n\\n**informers/internalinterfaces/factory_interfaces.go** — Internal interfaces used by generated informers: `SharedInformerFactory` (minimal), `NewInformerFunc`, `TweakListOptionsFunc`.\\n\\n**informers/generic.go** — `GenericInformer` interface and `genericInformer` for untyped resource access via `ForResource()`.\\n\\n**informers/*/interface.go and informers/*/*/*.go** — Generated per-resource informers for all Kubernetes API groups (admissionregistration, apps, autoscaling, batch, certificates, coordination, core, discovery, events, extensions, flowcontrol, networking, node, policy, rbac, resource, scheduling, storage, storagemigration). Each resource file implements a typed informer that calls `factory.InformerFor()` with a `NewInformerFunc` that creates a `NewFilteredListWatchFromClient` and calls `NewSharedIndexInformer`.\\n\\n## Specialized Factories\\n\\n**dynamic/dynamicinformer/informer.go** — `DynamicSharedInformerFactory` for unstructured dynamic client informers.\\n**dynamic/dynamicinformer/interface.go** — `DynamicSharedInformerFactory` interface.\\n**metadata/metadatainformer/informer.go** — `metadataSharedInformerFactory` for metadata-only informers.\\n**metadata/metadatainformer/interface.go** — `SharedInformerFactory` interface for metadata informers.\\n\\nAll these files exist both in `kubernetes/client-go` (standalone) and mirrored in `kubernetes/kubernetes` under `staging/src/k8s.io/client-go/`.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":1,"cache_creation_input_tokens":255,"cache_read_input_tokens":37862,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":255,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":0},"output_tokens":8,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"b61824d2-9d48-4dad-bdbf-62d45a0ddf2d","uuid":"66886e6c-1cf3-4b1b-93c5-8bd33195ec67"}

 \"text\": \"The SharedInformer factory and cache sync mechanism in kubernetes/kubernetes (and kubernetes/client-go) is implemented across several interconnected packages:\\n\\n## Core Cache Infrastructure (tools/cache/)\\n\\n**shared_informer.go** — The heart of the implementation. Defines the `SharedInformer` and `SharedIndexInformer` interfaces, and `sharedIndexInformer` struct which embeds a `controller`, a local `indexer` (store), and a `sharedProcessor` for fan-out event delivery. Key functions: `NewSharedIndexInformer`, `WaitForCacheSync`, `WaitForNamedCacheSync`. The `Run()` method starts the controller and processor; `HasSynced()` delegates to the underlying controller/DeltaFIFO.\\n\\n**controller.go** — Defines the `Controller` interface and its `controller` implementation. `controller.Run()` creates a `Reflector`, runs it against a `DeltaFIFO`, and runs `processLoop()` which calls `Pop` on the DeltaFIFO, dispatching to `ProcessFunc` (which is `sharedIndexInformer.HandleDeltas`). `processDeltas()` applies add/update/delete events to the local store and notifies handlers.\\n\\n**reflector.go** — Implements `Reflector` which drives the list-watch loop. `ListAndWatch()` does a full List to populate the store (via `DeltaFIFO.Replace`), then enters a Watch loop streaming incremental events. Handles resync, resource version management, and bookmark tracking.\\n\\n**listwatch.go** — Defines the `ListerWatcher` interface and `ListWatch` struct that wraps typed client functions. `NewListWatchFromClient` / `NewFilteredListWatchFromClient` build `ListWatch` objects from a typed REST client.\\n\\n**store.go** — Defines the `Store` interface and `cache` struct (the local in-memory store). `NewIndexer` creates an indexed store backed by `threadSafeMap`. `MetaNamespaceKeyFunc` is the default keying function.\\n\\n**thread_safe_store.go** — `ThreadSafeStore` / `threadSafeMap` provide the thread-safe in-memory map with secondary index support (`storeIndex`).\\n\\n**delta_fifo.go** — `DeltaFIFO` is the queue between the Reflector (producer) and the controller processLoop (consumer). `Replace()` does the initial sync from the List call; `Add/Update/Delete` handle watch events. `HasSynced()` tracks whether the initial list has been fully processed.\\n\\n**index.go** — Defines `Indexer` interface, `IndexFunc`, `MetaNamespaceIndexFunc`, `Indexers`, `Indices`, and `Index` types for secondary indexing.\\n\\n**synctrack/synctrack.go** — `AsyncTracker` and `SingleFileTracker` track per-item and global sync status, used by `sharedIndexInformer` to implement `HasSynced()`.\\n\\n## Factory Implementation (informers/)\\n\\n**informers/factory.go** — Implements `SharedInformerFactory` and the concrete `sharedInformerFactory`. `NewSharedInformerFactory` / `NewSharedInformerFactoryWithOptions` create the factory. `InformerFor()` registers or retrieves a `SharedIndexInformer` for a given object type, ensuring deduplication. `Start()` launches all registered informers. `WaitForCacheSync()` waits for all started informers to complete their initial list sync.\\n\\n**informers/internalinterfaces/factory_interfaces.go** — Internal interfaces used by generated informers: `SharedInformerFactory` (minimal), `NewInformerFunc`, `TweakListOptionsFunc`.\\n\\n**informers/generic.go** — `GenericInformer` interface and `genericInformer` for untyped resource access via `ForResource()`.\\n\\n**informers/*/interface.go and informers/*/*/*.go** — Generated per-resource informers for all Kubernetes API groups (admissionregistration, apps, autoscaling, batch, certificates, coordination, core, discovery, events, extensions, flowcontrol, networking, node, policy, rbac, resource, scheduling, storage, storagemigration). Each resource file implements a typed informer that calls `factory.InformerFor()` with a `NewInformerFunc` that creates a `NewFilteredListWatchFromClient` and calls `NewSharedIndexInformer`.\\n\\n## Specialized Factories\\n\\n**dynamic/dynamicinformer/informer.go** — `DynamicSharedInformerFactory` for unstructured dynamic client informers.\\n**dynamic/dynamicinformer/interface.go** — `DynamicSharedInformerFactory` interface.\\n**metadata/metadatainformer/informer.go** — `metadataSharedInformerFactory` for metadata-only informers.\\n**metadata/metadatainformer/interface.go** — `SharedInformerFactory` interface for metadata informers.\\n\\nAll these files exist both in `kubernetes/client-go` (standalone) and mirrored in `kubernetes/kubernetes` under `staging/src/k8s.io/client-go/`.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
